< name>
Jerrold Kazynski< /name>
<time>1582601785862< /time><rate>5</rate>< text>
Tackle Box opened shortly after two new water storage reservoirs were created in the early 1970s on the Fresno and Chowchilla Rivers, the way I remember it.

Fishing supplies of live bait, worms, some rods & reels were in stock. Their inventory now includes a beer vault, some wines and distilled liquors, snacks and general camping supplies and gasoline.

Their store is typically well stocked, and their usually lowest price in town for Regular gas keeps the customers happy.

On your next trip through Madera to Eastman Lake or Hensley Lake, get a fill-up and necessities at the original Tackle Box.<//text>

Great people, great service and they are honest and upfront with you. I broke my phone quite a few times (Google pixel 2 XL) with my broken screen and the back black glass portion of the phone. <Rating>5<//Rating><Text>So, I was walking actually rushing from the MUNI stop to Fix My Phone SF which to my surprise was only a half block away yesterday evening around 6:00 P.M.  Remind you the establishment closes at 5:00P.M. Another piece of information is the establishment also sells, rents and fixes bikes.  That's the reason I was heading to this location. I work for Postmates and they offer a great deal on leasing a genZe electric bike worth over $3,000 which Fix My phone SF is a distributor for them. Back to the story. When I got to the door it was locked. I knocked not once not twice but three times. No one answered so I thought they were gone for the evening but to what my wondering eyes should appear a gentleman walking a beautiful Maltice and no he wasn't with 8 tiny reindeer, down the sidewalk. When the gentleman approached he mentioned that the store looks as though it was closed. I kind of got the hint that he was the owner. He introduced himself as Michael. He then said "Well I'm kind of going home right now I have a really important date." He let me know that I would have to come back the following day. I explained to him that I just came from San Jose all the way to San Francisco to pick up a bike that I reserved through Postmates. I explained to him also that my transportation was chaotic and I should have been there five hours earlier but was held up because my dog was sick. He then stated "Come on in!" Let me tell you he was so generous and helpful and took his time to explain my lease and the specs on the bike knowing he had to be somewhere else. In fact he received a phone call during our transaction and I could hear the other person on the line requesting his presence. He explained to the person on the other line that he was going to finish helping me and get home as soon as possible. Now let me tell you that is great customer service to have someone go out of their way and stay a half an hour after they closed an hour before hand. I would highly recommend this place for your phone or bike needs and to top it off his prices are competitive to say in the least. What I mean by competitive is low price with quality work.  So the next time you need your phone fixed or you need to purchase a new one or rent a bike for a day stop by Fix My Phone SF located near the corner of Cole & Carl streets in the Haight Ashbury!</Text>< pics>

<Resp>None</Resp><rating>1</rating><date>1506369611000<//date>< Review>
Please note that this review is motivated by my feeling that this business deceived me multiple times and did not bother to offer an appropriate resolution when things went awry. This review has nothing to do with the fact that my phone, ultimately, wasn't fixed. It is unfortunate, because I have no issue supporting smaller businesses like this one.

The story: My iPhone 6 sustained water damage, which required a new screen and battery. I paid for the fix, and realized that the touch ID wasn't working. I took the phone back and paid additional money to get that fixed. A week later, I notice the screen was not properly installed so I went back to get that fixed.

Two weeks later I noticed the battery life was extremely poor when suddenly the phone shut off, and I was unable to restart it. Frustrated, I took the phone back to the store and the technician ran some tests and eventually were able to restart my phone. However, they were unable to discern what the actual issue was - which I found concerning.

Two weeks later, the same issue occurred. This time, the technician told me that my phone was beyond repair and the only "refund" they were willing to offer me was to sell me a used iPhone, and subtract all the fees I had already paid from the price of the phone, which I found incredibly unfair. And they were unwilling to budge, even on a partial refund. They pointed to the store policies, which I believe should only apply when the business does their job.

What's most concerning is that this business accepts cash only, and I now realize why: you cannot dispute this business with your credit card provider. Moreover, their warranty is only 90 days. It's all set up in their favor, and not in the consumer's favor at all. Further, I took my iPhone to two different repair places to run a diagnostic and both stores informed me that the store didn't use genuine parts, and as a result, those parts failed, thus ruining my iPhone.

Again, I'm not mad that my phone wasn't fixed - I'm mad that this business deceived me and were unwilling to operate on fair business practices.</Review>
